# <a name="release-notes-for-semi-annual-enterprise-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-103">有关半年企业频道的发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-103">Release notes for Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="630b9-104">我们为 Microsoft 365 企业应用版、Microsoft 365 商业应用版以及 Project 和 Visio 桌面应用的订阅版本提供了半年企业频道更新。这些发行说明提供了有关这些更新中所含新功能和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel updates for Microsoft 365 Apps for enterprise, Microsoft 365 Apps for business, and the subscription versions of the desktop apps for Project and Visio.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-105">我们正在对 Microsoft 365 应用的更新频道进行一些更改，包括添加新的更新频道（月度企业版频道）和更改现有更新频道的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-105">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-106">若要了解详细信息，请[阅读这篇文章](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-106">To learn more, [read this article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
>
>- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-107">如果半年企业频道上的用户从 Office 门户下载并在 Windows 10 上安装 Microsoft 365 应用版，现在默认情况下会包括 OneNote 2016。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-107">OneNote 2016 will now be included by default when a user on the Semi-Annual Enterprise Channel downloads and installs Microsoft 365 Apps on Windows 10 from the Office Portal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="630b9-110">*版本2008（内部版本13127.21064）*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-110">*Version 2008 (Build 13127.21064)*</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-113">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-113">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-114">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-114">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-115">**在“查询设计器”、“SQL 视图”和“关系”窗口中更高效地工作：** 右键单击表格，以对其进行打开、设计、调整大小和隐藏操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-115">**Be more productive working in Query Designer, SQL view, and the Relationships window:** Right-click a table to open, design, size, and hide it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-116">在 SQL 视图中搜索和替换文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-116">Search and replace text in SQL View.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-117">在“关系”窗口中选择多个表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-117">Select multiple tables in the Relationships window.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-118">**单击几下即可添加表：** 使用“添加表”任务窗格（在你工作时一直打开）向关系和查询添加表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-118">**Add tables with fewer clicks:** Use the Add Tables task pane, which stays open while you work, to add tables to relationships and queries.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-119">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-119">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/56eb7df2-8a52-4e90-a7e0-8f891a5c56bd)

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-120">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-120">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-121">**你喜爱的 Excel 函数运行速度更快：** SUMIFS、AVERAGEIFS、COUNTIFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS 函数运行速度比以往更快。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-121">**Your favorite Excel functions just got faster:** The SUMIFS, AVERAGEIFS, COUNTIFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS functions are much faster than ever before.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-122">更快达到底线。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-122">Get to the bottom line more quickly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-123">立即试用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-123">Try one now.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-124">**Realtimedata (RTD) 改进：** 在 Office 365 版本 2002 每月频道或更高版本中，Excel 的 RealTimeData (RTD) 函数要比 Excel 2010 计算电子表格中的数据的速度快得多。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-124">**Realtimedata (RTD) improvements:** In Office 365 version 2002 monthly channel and later, Excel's RealTimeData (RTD) function is much faster than Excel 2010 calculating data in the spreadsheet.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-125">我们在其基本内存和数据结构中删除瓶颈，并使其变得线程安全，这能允许其在 多线程计算 (MTR) 的所有可用线程上进行计算。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-125">We removed bottlenecks in its underlying memory and data structures as well as made it thread-safe to allow  it to be calculated on all available threads of Multithreaded recalculation (MTR).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-126">**改进的地图图表：** 我们改进了地图图表，将其与 Excel 的地理数据类型相集成，可显示有关地图位置的丰富信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-126">**Improved map charts:** We've made map charts better by integrating them with Excel's Geographic Data Types, which can reveal rich information about your mapped locations.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-127">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-127">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-128">**选取完美颜色：** 使用十六进制颜色代码选择字体和文本突出显示等所需的精确颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-128">**Pick the perfect color:** Use hex color codes to choose exactly the color you want for your font, text highlight, and more.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-129">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-129">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-130">**在 Excel 中从 Power BI 中的数据集创建数据透视表：** 你可以在 Excel 中创建连接到 Power BI 中存储的数据集的数据透视表，只需点击几下鼠标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-130">**Create PivotTables from Datasets in Power BI within Excel:** You can create PivotTables in Excel that are connected to datasets stored in Power BI with a few clicks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-131">这样做可以让你更好地利用数据透视表和 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-131">Doing this allows you get the best of both PivotTables and Power BI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-132">使用数据透视表从你的安全的 Power BI 数据集计算、总结和分析数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-132">Calculate, summarize, and analyze your data with PivotTables from your secure Power BI datasets.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-133">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-133">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/31444a04-9c38-4dd7-9a45-22848c666884)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-134">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-134">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/11/use-power-bi-data-in-excel/)</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-135">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-135">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-136">**选取完美颜色：** 使用十六进制颜色代码选择字体和文本突出显示等所需的精确颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-136">**Pick the perfect color:** Use hex color codes to choose exactly the color you want for your font, text highlight, and more.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-137">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-137">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-138">**改进日历：** 可查看视觉对象更新，以便更轻松地扫描日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-138">**Calendar gets a makeover:** See visual updates that make your calendar easier to scan.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-139">了解更多详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-139">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/1c04e438-d84a-44fc-a404-170c9007e65c)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-140">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/13/outlooks-calendar-gets-a-refresh/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-140">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/13/outlooks-calendar-gets-a-refresh/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-141">**共享日历更新速度更快：** 对于 Office 365 中的共享日历，Outlook 可以使用 REST API 更新这些日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-141">**Shared calendar updates just got faster:** For shared calendars in Office 365, Outlook can update these calendars using the REST API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-142">打开预览，更快速、更可靠地更新共享日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-142">Turn on the preview for faster and more reliable updates to shared calendars.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-143">**将电子邮件拖动到你拥有的组：** 通过从收件箱中拖动来移动和复制邮件和对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-143">**Drag email to a group you own:** Move and copy messages and conversations by dragging them from your inbox.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-144">将与所有组成员共享你拖动的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-144">Messages you drag will be shared with all group members.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-145">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/02/drag-messages-from-your-personal-inbox-to-the-group-mailbox/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-145">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/03/02/drag-messages-from-your-personal-inbox-to-the-group-mailbox/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-146">**不退出收件箱加入会议：** 无需切换至日历以加入联机会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-146">**Join meetings without leaving your inbox:** No need to switch to your calendar to join online meetings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-147">通过固定日历至待办事项窗格，只需单机一次即可加入任何会议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-147">With the Calendar pinned to the To-Do pane, join any meeting with just one click.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-148">**强制 wifi 网络新体验：** 是否已加入需要使用网页登录的 wifi 网络？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-148">**New experience for captive wifi networks:** Have you ever joined a wifi network that required a web page to sign in with?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-149">现在，Outlook 检测到这一点，帮助你进行连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-149">Outlook now detects this and helps you get connected.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-150">在[博客文章](https://insider.office.com/zh-CN/blog/outlook-on-public-wi-fi-networks-just-got-easier)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-150">See details in [blog post](https://insider.office.com/zh-CN/blog/outlook-on-public-wi-fi-networks-just-got-easier)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-151">**搜索某个人时获取电子邮件建议：** 在“搜索”框中键入某人姓名时，最相关的电子邮件信息将包含在搜索建议中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-151">**Get email suggestions when you search for a person:** When you type a person’s name in the Search box, the most relevant email messages will be included with your search suggestions.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-152">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-152">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/d824d1e9-a255-4c8a-8553-276fb895a8da)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-153">**更好的结果 - 瞬间完成：** 我们更新了搜索体验，使其更加智能、更快速，并且比以往更可靠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-153">**Better results—in a jiffy:** We've updated the Search experience to make it smarter, faster, and more reliable than ever.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-154">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-154">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/96fee452-80cd-492d-a35c-5c37584b416b)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-155">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-155">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-156">**GIF 瞬间完成：** 一幻灯片、一帧。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-156">**GIFs in a jiffy:** One slide, one frame.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-157">轻松在 PowerPoint 中创建循环 GIF。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-157">Easily create looping GIFs in PowerPoint.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-158">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-158">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/a598753e-92de-4f1b-8393-714db4d334b4)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-159">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/12/30/create-animated-gifs-using-powerpoint/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-159">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/12/30/create-animated-gifs-using-powerpoint/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-160">**指向幻灯片的链接：** 让同事参与幻灯片的创作，让其直接转到你需要帮助的幻灯片上。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-160">**Link to a slide:** Ask a colleague to contribute to your slide deck, and start them directly on the slide you need help with.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-161">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-161">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/4f5f3d5e-1674-4742-8cf1-9623050c19ef)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-162">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/12/share-a-link-to-a-specific-slide/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-162">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/12/share-a-link-to-a-specific-slide/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-163">**选取完美颜色：** 使用十六进制颜色代码选择字体和文本突出显示等所需的精确颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-163">**Pick the perfect color:** Use hex color codes to choose exactly the color you want for your font, text highlight, and more.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-164">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-164">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-165">**改进的地图图表：** 我们改进了地图图表，将其与 Excel 的地理数据类型相集成，可显示有关地图位置的丰富信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-165">**Improved map charts:** We've made map charts better by integrating them with Excel's Geographic Data Types, which can reveal rich information about your mapped locations.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-166">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-166">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-167">**更好的图表：** 有了更好的连接器和更流程的墨迹转换过程，你可以更轻松用墨迹表达你的想法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-167">**Better diagrams:** With better connectors and a smoother ink conversion process you can ink your ideas more confidently.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-168">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-168">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/0740dec3-6291-4c1f-8baa-011d18449919)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-169">**改进了 PowerPoint 的流视频性能：** 我们对 Microsoft Stream 视频的回放性能进行了改进，以最小化视频加载时间，创造流畅的观看体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-169">**Improved Stream video performance in PowerPoint:** We’ve made improvements to the playback performance of Microsoft Stream videos to minimize video loading time and create a smooth viewing experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-170">使用来自 Microsoft Stream 的企业视频来创建更好的演示文稿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-170">Use your corporate videos from Microsoft Stream to create better presentations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-171">**使用 @提及功能引起他人的注意：** 在批注中使用 @提及，以在需要同事的意见时让他们知悉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-171">**Get their attention with @mentions:** Use @mentions in comments to let co-workers know when you need their input.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-172">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-172">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/644bf689-31a0-4977-a4fb-afe01820c1fd)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-173">**演示时同步所做的更改：** 即使演示文稿处于幻灯片放映模式，只要进行了更改就同步这些更改。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-173">**Synchronize changes while you are presenting:** Synchronize changes whenever they are made even when the presentation is in slide show mode.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-174">了解更多详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-174">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5a2921a9-97d4-436b-b0cd-295dfe2236bb)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-175">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-175">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/04/08/synchronize-changes-while-presenting/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-176">**批注**：PowerPoint 中新的批注体验使你可以快速、轻松地发现批注并将其添加到文档中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-176">**Comments:** The new commenting experience in PowerPoint allows you to quickly and easily discover and add comments to your documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-177">通过批注锚定、解决、任务、改进的提及通知等新功能实现协作工作流现代化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-177">Modernize your collaboration workflows with new features like comment anchoring, resolve, tasks, improved mention notifications, and much more.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-178">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-178">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/c0aa37bb-82cb-414c-872d-178946ff60ec)

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-179">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-179">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-180">**用套索选择墨迹：**“绘图”选项卡上的“套索”工具可帮助你选择用墨迹绘制的对象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-180">**Lasso your ink:** The Lasso tool on the Draw tab helps you select objects drawn with ink.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-181">选择单独的笔划或整个字。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-181">Select individual strokes, or whole words.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-182">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-182">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/6d76c674-7f4b-414d-b67f-b3ffef6ccf53)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-183">**选取完美颜色：** 使用十六进制颜色代码选择字体和文本突出显示等所需的精确颜色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-183">**Pick the perfect color:** Use hex color codes to choose exactly the color you want for your font, text highlight, and more.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-184">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-184">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/02/19/hex-color-values-in-color-picker/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-185">**改进的地图图表：** 我们改进了地图图表，将其与 Excel 的地理数据类型相集成，可显示有关地图位置的丰富信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-185">**Improved map charts:** We've made map charts better by integrating them with Excel's Geographic Data Types, which can reveal rich information about your mapped locations.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-186">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-186">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-187">**屏幕阅读器中的操作确认：** 操作的确认是辅助功能一项重要的要求。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-187">**Confirmation of action in screen readers:** Confirmation of action is an important accessibility requirement.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-188">随着 Windows 引入新的通知 API ，我们现在可以提醒屏幕阅读器用户的操作成功情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-188">With the introduction of a new Notification API from Windows, we are now able to alert screen reader users about the success of their actions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-189">剪切、复制、粘贴、加粗、斜体、下划线、撤消、重做、自动更正、自动大小写等功能，现在都已向Win32 Word"讲述人"用户公布。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-189">Cut, copy, paste, bold, italic, underline, undo, redo, auto corrections, and auto-capitalizations are now all announced to Narrator users in Win32 Word.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-190">若要启用此功能，请按 windows + ctrl + enter 启用 "讲述人"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-190">To enable this feature, turn on Narrator by pressing windows + ctrl + enter.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-191">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/05/confirmation-of-action-in-word-for-windows/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-191">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2020/06/05/confirmation-of-action-in-word-for-windows/)</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-207">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-207">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-208">处于只读模式的工作簿可能已发生自动文档分类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-208">Automatic document classification may have occurred for workbooks that were in read-only mode.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-209">修复了当你已从帐户注销时尝试创建数据连接时可能发生的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-209">Fixed an issue that could happen when trying to create a data connection if you have signed out from your account.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-210">修复了 PivotDateFilter API 中“Before”和“After”筛选条件相互的颠倒的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-210">Fixed a bug with PivotDateFilter APIs in which 'Before' and 'After' filter conditions were reversed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-211">解决了在试图将数据透视表插入图表工作表时 Excel 可能意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-211">Addressed an issue where Excel may close unexpectedly when attempting to insert PivotTables into a chart sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-212">修复了以下问题：无法编辑从 Project 计划导出的数据透视表，并且无法保存相同情况下的工作簿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-212">Fixed an issue where pivot tables could not be edited and workbooks could not be saved if they were exported from Project plan.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-214">我们修复了以下问题：在某些情况下，在只读模式下打开文件时，会显示多个消息栏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-214">We fixed an issue where in some cases, multiple message bars were appearing when a file was opened in read-only mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-216">修正了只读书籍在打开时不再刷新数据透视表数据的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-216">Fixed an issue where read-only books would no longer refresh pivot table data when opened.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-217">此更改提供了对以下问题的修复：当从OneDrive本地同步文件夹插入文件时，Excel "插入对象 "不显示正确的图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-217">This change provides a fix for the following issue: Excel "Insert Object" does not show correct icon when inserts a file from OneDrive local sync folder.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-218">我们修复了以下问题：当发生组策略对象更新（例如，通过远程组策略刷新）时，Excel 会停止运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-218">We fixed an issue where Excel would stop working when there is a Group Policy Object update (e.g. via Remote Group Policy Refresh) during multithreaded recalc.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-220">当从 Excel 中复制内容并使用“嵌入”选项粘贴到 PowerPoint 时，改进了 PowerPoint 中的文本间距调整。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-220">Improved text kerning in PowerPoint when when content is copied from Excel and pasted into PowerPoint with the Embed option.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-226">修复了在使用某些Windows安全漏洞保护设置（SimExec、CallerCheck）时，Excel无法启动或意外崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-226">Fixes an issue where Excel would fail to launch or crash unexpectedly if certain Windows Security exploit protection settings (SimExec, CallerCheck) are in use</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-228">修复了用户无法修改数据透视表筛选器的问题，因为它被设置为在 Analysis Services 数据库中已不存在的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-228">We fixed an issue where users could not modify a PivotTable filter because it was set to a value that was no longer present in an Analysis Services database.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-229">修复了Excel在冻结工作表首行后使用快速分析时可能会意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-229">Fixed an issue where Excel could close unexpectedly when using the Quick Analysis after freezing the top row of the sheet.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-230">解决了某些函数在加载工作簿后可能出现错误结果的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-230">We fixed an issue where certain functions would have an incorrect result after loading a workbook.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-231">解决了与 XLAM 加载项引用和命名范围相关的应用程序意外终止的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-231">We fixed an issue where the application would terminate unexpectedly which was related to XLAM add-in references and named ranges.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-232">我们解决了以下问题：使用宏设置区域的 FormulaR1C1 属性时，如果图表工作表是活动工作表，则单元格引用将不正确。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-232">We fixed an issue where using a macro to set the FormulaR1C1 property for a range, the cell references would be incorrect if a chart sheet was the active sheet.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-234">修复了将 Office 语言设置为西班牙语时出现的问题，在有问题的情况下，数据验证列表可能不会显示列表中的所有项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-234">Fixed an issue when the Office language was set to Spanish, in which data validation lists may not show all the items in the list.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-236">修正了以下问题：保存到 SharePoint / OneDrive 时，自定义功能区标签的CustomUI XML被删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-236">Fixed an issue which caused CustomUI XML for a custom ribbon tab to be removed when saving to SharePoint/OneDrive.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-237">修正了团队共享 Excel 窗口时，使用Ctrl+Shift+箭头键滚动后Excel可能会无法响应的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-237">Fixed an issue where Excel could become unresponsive after using Ctrl+Shift+Arrow keys to scroll when the Excel window is shared through Teams.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-238">修复了以下问题：在某些情况下，单击指向同一工作簿内某个位置的超链接将导致工作簿被隐藏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-238">Fixed an issue where in some cases, clicking a hyperlink to a place within the same workbook will cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-239">Application.Evaluate (VBA) 在某些情况下不能用于用户定义的函数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-239">Application.Evaluate (VBA) was not working for User-defined functions in some cases.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-240">在当前版本的 Excel 中打开在 Excel 2016 保存含有数字签名的工作簿时，可能会使签名无效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-240">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-241">修复了在复制包含数据透视表的工作表后，在某些情况下会导致Excel意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-241">Fixed an issue which would cause Excel to close unexpectedly in some cases after copying a sheet containing a PivotTable.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-242">修复了如果文件路径过长，重新打开文件后外部链接会停止工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-242">Fixed an issue where the external link stops working after the file is reopened if the file path is too long.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-243">修复了在使用实时数据和多线程重新计算功能时可能导致的应用程序意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-243">Fixed an issue when using real time data in conjunction with multithreaded recalc functionality could cause the application to close unexpectedly.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-244">解决了如果关闭了源代码簿，则外部链接不会在填充时更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-244">Addressed an issue where external links don't update on fill if the source book is closed.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-245">修复了如果工作簿包含使用 IFNA() 的公式，则可能导致有关损坏的工作簿警告的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-245">Fixed an issue that could cause a warning about a corrupt workbook if it contained formulas using IFNA().</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-246">我们修复了一个问题，现在 Power Pivot 将能够成功识别制表符分隔符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-246">We fixed an issue where Power Pivot will now successfully recognize tab delimiter.</span></span>


### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-247">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-247">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-248">通知用户有关 Microsoft OneNote 中的暂时调整的信息栏，可有助于提升全球范围内使用期间的同步和服务可用性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-248">Inform users through the InfoBar about temporary adjustments in Microsoft OneNote that will help improve sync and service availability during high worldwide usage.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-249">通过临时调整 OneNote 2016 中的同步频率，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-249">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily adjusting sync frequency in OneNote 2016.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-250">改进对共同创作状态的检测，以减少资源利用率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-250">Improved detection of co-authoring status to reduce resource utilization.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-251">通过临时更改页面版本历史记录的创建频率，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-251">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily altering how frequently page version histories are created.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-252">在 OneNote 2016 中，通过暂时将新的嵌入式附件的最大允许大小降低到 50 MB，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-252">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily reducing the maximum allowable size of new embedded attachments to 50MB in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-253">对于超出此限制的文件，用户可以选择将文件上传到 OneDrive 并将链接插入OneNote。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-253">For files that exceed this limit, users will have the option of uploading the file to OneDrive and inserting a link into OneNote.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-254">通过暂时禁用 OneNote 2016 中的应用内视频录制功能，提升了同步和服务稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-254">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily disabling in-app video recording in OneNote 2016.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-255">本地笔记本不受此措施影响。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-255">Local notebooks are not impacted by this measure.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-256">通过暂时禁用将页面移动到回收站来提升同步和服务器稳定性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-256">Improved sync and service stability by temporarily disabling moving pages into the recycle bin.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-257">希望删除页面的用户将改为显示一个对话框，询问用户是否想要永久删除页面。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-257">Users who want to delete a page will instead be shown a dialog asking if they'd want to permanently delete the page.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-258">我们修复了拼写菜单无法加载的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-258">We fixed an issue where the spelling menu was not loading.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-305">我们添加了一个 regkey，允许客户在 IDataObject 操作（例如，拖放、剪贴板）中禁用附件的 filetime 包含。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-305">We added a regkey that allows customers to disable filetime inclusion for attachments in IDataObject operations (i.e. drag drop, clipboard).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-306">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject  0 = 排除 filetime  1 =（默认）包含 filetime</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-306">HKCU\SOFTWARE\Microsoft\Office\16.0\Outlook\Attachments REG_DWORD IncludeFileTimesInDataObject  0 = filetimes are excluded  1 = (default) filetimes are included</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-309">我们修复了以下问题：设置 OME 配置时会在邮件项目上添加一个无关的附件，这会迫使 Outlook 对邮件进行加密，即使在服务端设置了 DecryptAttachmentsForEncryptOnly 选项也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-309">We fixed an issue where setting up OME Configuration was adding an extraneous attachments on the mail item which was forcing Outlook to Encrypt the message even though the DecryptAttachmentsForEncryptOnly option was setup on the service side.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-392">当用户在办公室的喷墨打印机上打印任何文档/文件，并且打印机墨水不足时，即使喷墨打印机不需要碳粉，也会显示 "碳粉不足 "或 "无碳粉 "的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-392">When the user prints any document/file on inkjet printers from Office and printer's ink is low, "Toner Low" or "No Toner" message will show, even though inkjet printers don't have toners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-393">将信息更改为显示 "碳粉/墨水不足" & "无碳粉/墨水"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-393">Changing message to display "Toner/ink Low" & "No toner/ink".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-394">我们通过设置Bing插件安装验证默认为真实，并使MSI返回成功视为安装成功，解决了ValidateInstall失败率问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-394">We have resolved the ValidateInstall fail rate issue by setting the Bing Addon install validation to true by default and considering the MSI return success as an install success.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-395">我们对新的 AppV51 进行了备份，以修复之前 AppV51 中的回归问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-395">We backported a new AppV51 drop to fix a regression in previous AppV51.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-396">解决了尝试硬链接符号链接时导致更新失败的即点即用问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-396">Fixed a Click-to-Run issue which was resulting in update failure when trying to hard link symbolic links.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-397">解决了使用 Microsoft 365 端点数据丢失防护利用 System Center Configuration Manager 或其他 Office Update 管理工具的商业客户的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-397">Addressed an issue for commercial customers who leverage System Center Configuration Manager or other management tool for the Office Update using Microsoft 365 Endpoint data loss prevention.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-398">修复了即使完成向完整产品的转换也导致显示运行时消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-398">Fixed an issue that caused a runtime message to show even though the transition to the full product is complete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-399">解决此问题的方法是确保服务会正确计算添加的产品。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-399">The fix for this issue was to ensure the service properly computed added products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-400">我们筛选掉了新添加的产品（确保这些产品同时存在于新配置中），并将其添加到现有产品发布 ID 的末尾。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-400">We filtered out the newly added products (ensuring that they exist in the new configuration as well) and added them to the end of existing Product release IDs.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-401">解决了用户发现 UI 元素或内容在某些条件下（尤其是在进出演示者视图或使用多个显示器时）不显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-401">We fixed an issue where users were seeing the UI elements or content not being displayed under certain conditions, in particular with coming in and out of Presenter View or using multiple monitors.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-402">此更改解决了与打开包含遗留图的文件相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-402">This change addresses an issue related to opening files containing legacy diagrams.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-403">此更改解决 SVG 回退代理导致访问违规的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-403">This change addresses an issue with SVG fallback proxy resulting in access violations.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-404">修复使用 GIF/动画模型 3D 时空闲的高 CPU 使用率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-404">Fixes high CPU usage on idle with GIF/animated model3D</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-405">此更改解决了加载和播放动画内容（如 Gif 或 3D 模型）时可能挂起的情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-405">This change addresses potential hangs when loading and playing animated content such as GIFs or 3D models.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-406">此更改解决了启动 Office 应用时由于无法加载 d2d1 而出现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-406">This change addresses a issue when launching Office apps due to failing to load d2d1.dll.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-407">当注册表键HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth被设置为零并且一个外接程序正在被激活时，windows中的office主机意外关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-407">The office host was  close unexpectedly in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-408">此更改可修复此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-408">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-409">解决了 Office 加载项的消息传递 API 无法正常工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-409">Fix an issue that the Messaging API for Office Add-ins is not working.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-410">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-410">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-411">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中的一个问题，即在运行时可能无法正确找到所含引用可通过搜索 PATH 环境变量中指定的位置找到的 Visual Basic for Applications 项目，从而导致 VBA 运行时错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-411">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Office where Visual Basic for Applications projects with references that are expected to be found by searching locations specified in the PATH environment variable may not be found properly at runtime, leading to VBA runtime errors.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-412">此修复程序解决了阻止同时使用密码限制访问和保护文件的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-412">This fix resolves an error which occurs preventing both restricting access and protecting files with a password simultaneously.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-413">解决了从应用中拖动某些内容时可能导致意外关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-413">Resolved an issue that may have caused an unexpected closure when dragging some content from the app.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-478">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-478">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-479">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-479">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-480">只要满足 Access 数据库的指导原则和要求，应该就不会再在 64 位版本的 Access 上收到“查询太复杂”或有关超出系统资源的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-480">You should no longer receive a "Query is too complex" or a system resource exceeded error on your 64-bit version of Access, as long as you are meeting Access database guidelines and requirements.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-481">当你决定在查询设计器之后使用过滤器功能时，数据库应该就不会再崩溃了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-481">Once you decide to use our filter feature after our query designer, your database should no longer crash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-482">请进行相应检查。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-482">Please check accordingly.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-483">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-483">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-484">修复了用户无法修改数据透视表筛选器的问题，因为它被设置为在 Analysis Services 数据库中已不存在的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-484">We fixed an issue where users could not modify a PivotTable filter because it was set to a value that was no longer present in an Analysis Services database.</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-485">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-485">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-486">通过模板创建的新演示文稿可能会继承妨碍良好的共同创作体验的设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-486">New presentations created from a template could inherit a setting that prevented  a good co-authoring experience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-487">此修补程序可确保在这种情况下清除该设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-487">This fix ensures that the setting is cleared in this case.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-488">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-488">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-489">我们解决了以下问题：打开包含分页符和列的文档时，用户可能遇到错误消息“你已超出 Microsoft Word 所支持的最大页面数目，或文档可能已损坏”</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-489">We fixed an issue which when opening documents with page breaks and columns, user might encountered an error message, " You have exceeded the maximum number of pages allowed by Microsoft Word supported, or the document may be damaged"</span></span>


### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-490">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-490">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-491">当用户在办公室的喷墨打印机上打印任何文档/文件，并且打印机墨水不足时，即使喷墨打印机不需要碳粉，也会显示 "碳粉不足 "或 "无碳粉 "的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-491">When the user prints any document/file on inkjet printers from Office and printer's ink is low, "Toner Low" or "No Toner" message will show, even though inkjet printers don't have toners.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-492">将信息更改为显示 "碳粉/墨水不足" & "无碳粉/墨水"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-492">Changing message to display "Toner/ink Low" & "No toner/ink".</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-550">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-550">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-551">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-551">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-552">**快速查找链接的表格：** 新的“搜索”框使查找链接的表格成为一项轻松的乐事。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-552">**Find linked tables fast:** Our new search box makes finding linked tables a breeze.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-553">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-553">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/1d9346d6-953d-4f85-a9ce-4caec2262797)

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-554">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-554">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-555">**更快的文件共享：** 直接从最近使用的文件列表中共享文档，而无需打开文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-555">**Faster file sharing:** Share your documents right from the recently used list without having to open the file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-556">**数据可视化工具加载项：** 从 Excel 中快速创建 Visio 流程图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-556">**Data visualizer add-in:** Quickly create Visio flowcharts from Excel.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-557">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-557">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/bee3b5aa-aaaf-4401-acc6-276b711c763c)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-558">**创建更易于访问的 PDF：** 创建一个 PDF，辅助功能检查器将会在你进行保存前指出要修复的辅助功能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-558">**Create more accessible PDFs:** Create a PDF and the accessibility checker will point out accessibility issues to fix before you save.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-559">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-559">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/064625e0-56ea-4e16-ad71-3aa33bb4b7ed)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-560">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/08/13/accessible-pdfs-made-easier/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-560">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/08/13/accessible-pdfs-made-easier/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-561">**更多符合你心情的图标：** 我们添加了 300 多个新图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-561">**More icons to match your mood:** We've added over 300 new icons.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-562">可在“插入”>“图标”中找到它们。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-562">Find them at Insert > Icons.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-563">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-563">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/3b179567-785e-42ac-8544-ec4ee5ebf1c8)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-564">**将文件转换为改进辅助功能：** 将文件升级到新式格式，使其更易于所有人访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-564">**Convert files to improve accessibility:** Upgrade your files to the modern format to make them more accessible for everyone.</span></span><br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-565">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/10/07/take-full-advantage-of-accessibility-in-office-documents/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-565">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/10/07/take-full-advantage-of-accessibility-in-office-documents/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-566">**关注剩余待办事项：** 选择“解决”可折叠评论并突出显示待处理的项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-566">**Focus on what's left to do:** Select Resolve to collapse comments and make open items stand out.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-567">**键入可返回多个值的公式：** 现可键入返回多个值的公式，它们将自动溢出到相邻的单元格中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-567">**Type a formula that returns multiple values:** Quickly type a formula that returns multiple values, and they'll automatically spill into the neighboring cells.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-568">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-568">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5c2c9cbb-def8-409a-b380-2fbf91b20aa3)<br /><span data-ttu-id="630b9-569">在[博客文章](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/06/13/dynamic-arrays-and-new-functions-in-excel/)中查看详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-569">See details in [blog post](https://blog-insider.office.com/2019/06/13/dynamic-arrays-and-new-functions-in-excel/)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-570">**不再跳转到浏览器：** 由你决定如何打开 Office 文档链接：在浏览器还是在应用中打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-570">**No more bouncing to the browser:** You decide how links to Office documents open: in the browser or in the app.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-597">**Outlook 中的插入链接菜单将插入包含租户管理员定义的权限的链接：** Outlook 插入链接 MRU 中的链接将插入仅对已经拥有权限的用户有效的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-597">**Insert Link Menu in Outlook will insert a link with permission defined by tenant admin:** A link from the Insert Link MRU in Outlook would insert a link that only worked for users who already had permissions to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-598">这通常会导致请求获得文档访问权限的用户之间发生往来电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-598">This often caused back and forth emails between users asking to be granted access to a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-599">我们已更新了此体验，现在该链接将通过租户管理员设置的默认权限进行插入。对于 MSIT，这“可供组织编辑”，因此收到以此方式共享的链接的所有内部用户都可以访问它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-599">We've updated this experience so now the link is inserted with the default permission set by the tenant admin. For MSIT this is "organization can edit" so all internal users who receive a link shared this way will be able to access it.</span></span>

### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-692">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-692">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-693">此更新修复了使用 ADODB 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-693">This update fixes an issue where using an ADODB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-694">VB 代码中的记录器对象可能会错误地报告错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-694">Recorder object in VB code may incorrectly report an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-695">Access 模板将不会再导致数据库中的附件列出现故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-695">Access templates should no longer cause attachment columns to fail within a database.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-696">在实例化模板后，你现在应该可以将附件字段添加到数据库中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-696">After instantiating a template, you should now be able to add an attachment field to your database.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-697">此更新修复了可能会导致 Microsoft Access 无法识别链接 SQL Server 表中的标识列的问题，该问题可能会导致行错误地被报告为已删除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-697">This update fixes an issue that can cause Microsoft Access to fail to identify an Identity Column in a linked SQL Server table, which can cause rows to be reported as deleted incorrectly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-698">此更新修复了 Microsoft Access 中的一个问题，该问题可能会导致运行更新查询或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 语句时出现“查询已损坏”错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-698">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error "Query is Corrupt" when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-699">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-699">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-700">加速加载本地 OneDrive 文件夹中提供的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-700">Speed up loading of files that are available on local OneDrive folder.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-701">修复了 CUBEVALUE 函数有时会返回错误结果的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-701">Fixed an issue where CUBEVALUE functions would sometimes return an incorrect result.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-702">解决了打开嵌入式工作簿时，未加载功能区自定义项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-702">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-703">在某些情况下，重新打开嵌入 Word 或 PowerPoint 的工作簿时，Excel 会崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-703">Excel would crash in certain cases when re-opening a workbook embedded in Word or PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-704">修复了未显示上下文菜单中的批注命令的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-704">Fixed an issue where comment commands in the context menu were not being displayed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-705">我们修复了数据透视图的右键单击菜单，以便启用“显示详细信息”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-705">We fixed the right click menu for Pivot Charts to enable the option to Show Details.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-706">解决了在无工作簿打开的情况下搜索最近使用的文件时可能导致出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-706">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-707">我们解决了在同一工作簿中单击带有书签的超链接会导致工作簿隐藏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-707">Fixed an issue where clicking a bookmarked hyperlink within the same workbook would cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-708">当另存为 CSV 文件时，在某些情况下，Excel 可能将所有列合并为一个列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-708">When saving as a CSV file, Excel could merge all columns into a single column in some cases.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-709">在受保护工作表中的某个区域内使用 Range.ClearContents 的时间可能比预期的要长。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-709">Using Range.ClearContents on a range in a protected sheet could take longer than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-710">修复了在“打印预览”中显示时表单控件中的文本缩放问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-710">Fixed a problem with scaling of text in form controls when displayed in Print Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-711">与功能区交互的 VBA 宏可能在 ScreenUpdating 意外设置为 True 的情况下运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-711">VBA macros that interact with the ribbon may run with ScreenUpdating set to True unexpectedly.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-712">修复了导致以下情形的问题：复制包含数据透视表的工作表后，在某些情况下 Excel 会崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-712">Fixed an issue which would cause Excel to crash in some cases after copying a sheet containing a PivotTable.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-715">修复了一个有关 VBA 的问题：将值写入某个区域可能比预期的要慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-715">Fixed an issue with VBA in which writing values to a range would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-716">从按颜色筛选的列复制的数据有时无法正确粘贴。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-716">Data copied from a column filtered by color sometimes would not paste properly.</span></span>

recurring meetings and appointments are displayed in the wrong timeslot for the year 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-768">此更改涉及到在巴西利亚时区设置的客户端以及在该时区设置的会议和约会。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-768">This change is relevant for clients set in the Brazilia time zone or for meetings and appointments set in that time zone.</span></span><br><br><span data-ttu-id="630b9-769">通过此更改，Outlook 可覆盖 Outlook 使用的特定时区设置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-769">This change allows Outlook to override certain time zone settings used by Outlook.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-770">若要调用时区覆盖，你必须为当前用户设置注册表项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-770">In order to invoke a time zone override you must set a registry key for the current user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-771">注册表项名称必须与时区的内部名称相匹配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-771">The registry key name must match the internal name of the time zone.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-772">该值表示将使用时区规则的年份代替有效年份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-772">The value indicates the time zone rule's year to be used in place of the effective year.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-773">例如，下面的注册表项替代值将使用 2020 年的 Brazilia 时区规则作为有效规则。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-773">For example, the following registry key override value will use the Brazilia time zone rule for the year 2020 as the effective rule.</span></span> <span ### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-854">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-854">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-855">修复了一个问题，即用户在大型 PowerPoint 文件上进行共同创作时遇到过多的网络和 CPU 使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-855">Fixed an issue where users can experience excessive network and CPU usage while coauthoring on large PowerPoint files.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-857">我们通过将后台的频道名称更新为 2020 年 1 月的分支中的新频道名称来解决此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-857">We resolved this issue by updating the channel names in the backstage to the new channel names in the January 2020 Fork.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-858">我们已修复此问题，接下来，如果设备是由策略管理的，则不会调用 DMS Audience API。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-858">We have fixed this issue and going forward, if a device is policy-managed, it will not call the DMS Audience API.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-859">解决了在单个事务中添加和删除应用时删除不完整的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-859">We have resolved the issue where there is an incomplete removal when adding and removing apps in a single transaction.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-860">修复了 ODT 和 GPO 更新截止时间设置中相对截止日期仅在第一次设置时起作用，而修复程序为后续更新启用相对截止日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-860">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-861">解决了 Office 更新可能已意外地从 Office CDN 而不是计划源（例如本地/网络共享或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置）下载文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-861">Resolves an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-862">修复了 ODT 和 GPO 更新截止时间设置中相对截止日期仅在第一次设置时起作用，而修复程序为后续更新启用相对截止日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-862">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-863">我们对新的 AppV51 进行了备份，以修复之前 AppV51 中的回归问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-863">We backported a new AppV51 drop to fix a regression in previous AppV51.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-864">我们已经解决了内部操作在失败时引发异常而不是进行记录并继续的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-864">We have resolved the issue where an internal operation was throwing an exception on failure instead of logging and continuing on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-865">受影响的用户将不再被阻止接收更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-865">The affected users will not be blocked from receiving updates anymore.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-866">我们的团队增加了客户端支持，可在半年度企业预览版中报告 Office CDN 域上的遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-866">Our team has added client support for reporting telemetry on the Office CDN domains in Semi-Annual Enterprise Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-867">此更改解决了利用 Intel 集成 GPU 的图形适配器所报告的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-867">This change addresses reported problems with graphics adaptors that leverage the Intel Integrated GPU.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-868">此更改可确保草绘轮廓在功能区中正常工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-868">This change ensures Sketched outline works properly in the ribbon.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-869">修复了从具有某些特定代理配置的本地位置打开文件时出现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-869">Fixed an issue while opening files from on-prem locations with some specific proxy configurations.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-870">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-870">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-871">修复了可在 Office 切换会话期间防止崩溃并提高用户体验可靠性的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-871">Fixed an issue that eliminates crashes during Office handoff sessions and improved reliability in the user experience.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-872">此 bug 将更新增强型配置服务 (ECS) url 终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-872">This bug updates the enhanced configuration service (ECS) url endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-873">调用此较新的终结点可以提高从 ECS 获取数据的成功率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-873">Calling this newer endpoint has a higher success rate for fetching from ECS.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-874">此更新修复了 Microsoft Outlook 在用户查看或撰写邮件时不显示当前敏感度标签的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-874">This update fixes an issue with Microsoft Outlook not displaying the current sensitivity label when viewing or composing messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-875">修复了从同一 SharePoint 库在 Word/Excel/PowerPoint 中打开多个文件时，只能打开第一个文件进行策略符合性扫描的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-875">Fixes an issue when multiple documents are open in Word/Excel/PowerPoint from the same SharePoint library, only the first document opened will be scanned for Policy compliance.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-876">为了保护 Office 客户的安全，现在仅使用 SHA-2 算法对 Microsoft Office 更新进行签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-876">To protect Office customers’ security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-877">当注册表键HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth被设置为零并且另外一个外接程序正在被激活时，windows中的office主机关闭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-877">The office host was closing in windows, when an add-in is being activated while the registry key  HKEY_CURRENT_USER\Software\Microsoft\Internet Explorer\Main\TabProcGrowth is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-878">此更改可修复此问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-878">This change would fix this issue.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-879">解决了可能无法正确启动 Access 和 Publisher（具体取决于安装的语言）的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-879">Resolved the issue where Access and Publisher might not boot correctly depending on which languages were installed.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-886">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-886">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-887">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-887">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-888">该更新修复了诸如“总和”等聚合可能将结果截断为整数值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-888">This update fixes an issue where aggregate like Sum may truncate the result to an integer value.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-889">该更新修复了包含对远程表（例如 SQL Server 表）的引用的联合查询可能导致 Access 关闭并重新启动的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-889">This update fixes an issue where a Union query that includes references to remote tables (e.g. SQL Server tables) may cause Access to close and restart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-890">此更新修复了 Microsoft Access 中的一个问题，该问题可能会导致运行更新查询或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 语句时出现“查询已损坏”错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-890">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error "Query is Corrupt" when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-891">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-891">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-892">荷兰语文档标题快捷键提示已更改为 Alt-G。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-892">Dutch keytip for document title has been changed to Alt-G.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-893">修复了 Excel 中的问题，其中分配给形状或表单控件的宏可能显示不正确的错误消息，或者可能在不正确的目标区域中工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-893">Fixed an issue in Excel where macros assigned to shapes or form controls may show incorrect error message, or may work on incorrect target ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-894">解决了一个“查找和替换”问题，即在找到第一个项目后它改变了对话框中焦点的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-894">Resolved an issue with Find and Replace that change where the focus was in the dialog after finding the first item.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-895">修复了在更改数据透视表的排序方式并在与其他用户进行共同创作会话期间刷新它时可能触发崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-895">This fixes an issue where changing the way a PivotTable is sorted and refreshing it while in a coauthoring session with other users could trigger a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-896">我们修复了当 OLAP 数据透视表的筛选器设置为已从多维数据集中删除的值时的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-896">We fixed a problem when the filter for an OLAP PivotTable was set to a value that had been removed from the cube.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-897">此更新修复了以下问题：当使用 VBA 向图表的页眉/页脚添加图像时，将会导致出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-897">This update fixes an issue that caused an error to occur whenever VBA was used to add an image to the header/footer of a chart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-898">我们修复了在更改系列集合时可能导致散点图无法正确呈现的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-898">We fixed an issue which could have caused scatter line charts from rendering properly when changing the series collection</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-899">修复了使用图表模板插入图表时预览中所用颜色的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-899">Fix to correct colors used in previews when inserting charts using chart templates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-900">解决了导致瀑布图和漏斗图无法与插入或删除单元格时的表格同步的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-900">Resolved an issue that caused Waterfall and Funnel charts to get out of sync with tables when cells were inserted or deleted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-901">已修复了 Excel 中的合并冲突问题，该问题会导致系统提示用户重新打开工作簿以使更改生效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-901">Fixed a merge conflict issue in Excel that would result in users being prompted to reopen workbook to pick up the changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-902">解决了导致激活最小化窗口的宏运行时错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-902">Resolved an issue that caused a macro run-time error activating minimized windows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-903">解决了打开嵌入式工作簿时，未加载功能区自定义项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-903">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-904">解决了在与其他人共同创作时导致表旁边的剪切和粘贴操作失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-904">Resolved an issue that caused cut and paste operations next to a table to fail when co-authoring with others.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-905">解决了在使用运行的宏更改自定义属性时导致共同创作中断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-905">Resolved an issue that caused co-authoring interruptions when changing custom properties with running macros.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-906">发生问题时，将无法从加载项打开的 WPF （Windows Presentation Foundation）窗体的组合框中选择项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-906">There was a problem in which you would be unable to select items from combo box of a WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) form that was opened by an add-in.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-907">解决了在无工作簿打开的情况下搜索最近使用的文件时可能导致出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-907">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-908">修复了在打印预览中或打印时分组框控件的边框不可见的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-908">Fixed an issue where the border of a Group Box control wasn't visible in print preview or when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-909">修复了当工作簿中存在外部链接时某些用户可能遇到多个弹出窗口的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-909">Fixed an issue where some users may have experienced multiple pop-up windows when external links were present in the workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-910">修复了用户在使用 VBA 宏清除某区域中的内容时可能遇到的性能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-910">Fixed a performance issue that users may have experienced when using a VBA macro to clear the contents of a range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-911">修复了一个有关 VBA 的问题：将值写入某个区域可能比预期的要慢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-911">Fixed an issue with VBA in which writing values to a range would be slower than expected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-912">解决了保存并重新打开文件时图表坐标轴上的“值交叉点”属性意外发生更改的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-912">Addresses an issue where the "Value Crosses At" property on chart axis unexpectedly changes when saving and re-opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-913">含有数字签名且在 Excel 2016 中保存的工作簿在当前版本的 Excel 中打开时，可能会使签名无效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-913">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-914">修复了删除包含合并单元格的列时导致性能降低的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-914">Fixed an issue which led to slow performance when deleting columns that contain merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-915">修复了在“打印预览”中显示时表单控件中的文本缩放问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-915">Fixed a problem with scaling of text in form controls when displayed in Print Preview.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-916">将按颜色筛选的数据复制到具有不同宽度的列时，不会粘贴这些值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-916">When copying data filtered by color to a column with a different width, the values would not be pasted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-917">修正了团队共享 Excel 窗口时，使用Ctrl+Shift+箭头键滚动后Excel可能会无法响应的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-917">Fixed an issue where Excel could become unresponsive after using Ctrl+Shift+Arrow keys to scroll when the Excel window is shared through Teams.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-918">修复了打印时窗体控件中的复选框缩放的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-918">Fixed a problem with the scaling of checkboxes in form controls when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-919">我们解决了在同一工作簿中单击带有书签的超链接会导致工作簿隐藏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-919">Fixed an issue where clicking a bookmarked hyperlink within the same workbook would cause the workbook to be hidden.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-920">尝试在新工作表上为使用旧版“共享工作簿”模式的工作簿列出更改时，可能会发生崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-920">A crash could occur when trying to list changes on a new sheet for a workbook using legacy "Shared Workbook" mode.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-921">某些区域设置的“文本分列”功能可能会失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-921">Text to Column functionality may fail for some locales.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-922">访问隐藏命名区域时，用户可能会遇到错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-922">Users may encounter an error when accessing a hidden named range.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-923">用户在使用部分非英文字符集保存更改时可能会出错。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-923">Users may encounter an error when saving changes while using some non-English character sets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-924">修复了以下问题：在保存包含图表的工作簿时，图表标题中的图像文件大小增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-924">Fixed an issue where the file size of images in chart headers increased when the workbook containing the chart was saved.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-925">异步用户定义函数的性能问题，该问题导致它们同步运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-925">Performance issue with Asynchronous User-Defined Functions that was causing them to be run Synchronously.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-926">显著提高了删除包含合并单元格的列时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-926">Significant improvements to the performance of deleting columns with merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-927">解决了在滚动后选择单元格时可能导致选择错误单元格的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-927">Resolved an issue where selecting a cell after scrolling could result in the wrong cell being selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-928">解决了 Lookup 函数可能返回错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-928">Resolved an issue where the Lookup function may return an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-929">修复了以下问题：在使所选区域与交叉引用的工作簿保持同步时，导致交叉引用工作簿中的 DBCS 字符出现损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-929">Fixed an issue that causes corruption of DBCS characters in cross referenced books by keeping the selection ranges in sync with the cross referenced book.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-930">解决了使用自动调整功能调整行高时复选框控件缩小的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-930">Resolved an issue that could cause check box controls to shrink when using autofit to adjust row height.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-931">当文件具有大量条件格式时，单击“字体颜色”按钮时会出现性能较低的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-931">Issue with slow performance on clicking on the Font Color button when a file has extensive conditional formatting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-932">我们修复了打印预览中的打印区域不正确的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-932">We fixed an issue where the print area in print preview was not correct.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-933">Excel 可能会在编辑不受信任的网络共享中的受保护文件时遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-933">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-934">我们显著提高了按颜色筛选的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-934">We have significantly improved the performance of filtering by color.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-935">解决了一个问题，当创建于早期版本的 Office 中的工作簿在当前版本的 Office 中打开时，可能会导致 Excel 挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-935">Resolved an issue where workbooks created in earlier versions of Office could cause Excel to hang when opened in current versions of Office.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-998">我们修复了将一个幻灯片从一个演示文稿复制到另一个演示文稿时，可能创建重复母版的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-998">We fixed an issue when copying a slide from one presentation to another might create duplicate masters.</span></span><br>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1000">修复了荧光笔问题：带有黑色荧光笔颜色的白色文本在打印后显示为灰度中的黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1000">Fixed an issue with highlighter : White texts with dark highlighter colors are printed as black in Grayscale.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1004">修复了以下问题：当逐步打开文件时，如果其中一张幻灯片包含多个嵌入式媒体流，则可能会出现问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1004">Fixed an issue that can occur when a file being opened incrementally contains a slide with more than one embedded media stream.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1005">我们修复了 Shape.Paste 方法的问题：当用户使用 Shape.Paste 方法复制和粘贴形状时，它会将所选内容更改为粘贴的形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1005">We fixed an issue with Shape.Paste method: when user copies and paste the shape using Shape.Paste method it changes the selection to the pasted shape.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1006">我们修复了第一次启动 PowerPoint 时可能不会显示不受信任的加载项的安全警告消息栏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1006">We fixed an issue where security warning message bar may not appear for untrusted add-ins on first launch of PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1007">修复了某些加载项会在图表中的形状周围引发意外错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1007">Fixed an issue where some add-ins would throw unexpected errors around shapes in charts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1008">防止 PowerPoint 用户在尝试联机演示时遇到错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1008">Prevents PowerPoint users from running into error when trying to Present Online.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1009">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1009">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1010">修复了 Windows 7 上的用户能够从 Project Web App 和 SharePoint 网站打开项目的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1010">Fixed an issue to enable users on Windows 7 to be able to open projects from Project Web App and SharePoint sites.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1011">发现了用户在打开只读项目时可能会收到几则消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1011">Identified an issue where users could get several messages when opening a read-only project.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1012">“全部调配”命令不能正确解决资源的过度分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1012">Level All command doesn't properly resolve a resource overallocation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1013">如果你的任务分配为零工作，该任务可能无法标记为已完成，并且始终显示为 99%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1013">An assignment with zero work on a task, the task may be unable to be marked complete and will always show up at 99%.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1014">修复了以下问题：由于基准日历发生更改时未更新资源日历，时间表与项目计划之间的实际工时可能不同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1014">Fixed an issue where actual work may be different between the timesheet and project plan due to resource calendars not being updated when the base calendar changes.</span></span>
