- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1021">我们修复了在使用 Deskjet 打印机打印时可能导致缩放问题的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1021">We fixed an issue which could have caused scaling issues when printing to Deskjet printers</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1022">修复了使文本适应表格的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1022">We fixed an issue in Fit Text in Table.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1023">我们修复了跟踪更改有时会陷入无限循环的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1023">We fixed an issue in track changes that sometimes go into infinite loop.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1024">我们修复了以下问题：在某些情况下，保存现有文件始终会导致显示“另存为”对话框，而该文件从不实际保存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1024">We fixed an issue where in some cases, saving an existing file always causes the Save As dialog and the file never actually saves.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1025">我们修复了将 2 个文档合并为一个文档时出现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1025">We fixed an issue when merging 2 documents into one document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1026">修复了受编辑保护的文档的“比较”功能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1026">Fixed an issue with Compare feature for documents that were protected for editing.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1027">修复了应用可能会在关闭时挂起的各种问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1027">Fixes various issues where the app may hang on shutdown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1028">还修复了某些加载项相关的崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1028">Also fixes certain add-in related crashes.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1029">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1029">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1030">修复了将采用平假名和日语汉字的新纪元名称“Reiwa”错误地标识为拼写错误或不符合语法的表达式的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1030">Fixed an issue of incorrectly identifying the new era name “Reiwa” in Hiragana and Kanji as a misspelled or ungrammatical expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1031">修复了一个问题，该问题导致用户在尝试共享存储在 SharePoint 2016 上的文件时收到消息“抱歉，无法我们共享此内容”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1031">Fixed an issue which caused users to get this message "Sorry, something is preventing us from sharing this" when trying to share files stored on SharePoint 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1032">修复了可能会导致 PowerPoint 中涉及共同创作和脱机编辑的会话中数据丢失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1032">Fixed issue that could cause data loss in sessions that involved both coauthoring and offline editing in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1033">此修复可解决用户打开文件时可能遇到的崩溃问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1033">This is a fix for a crash that users could hit on opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1034">在某些情况下，同步引擎支持的 sharepoint 文件可能显示“已保存”，但并未真正保存任何更改，导致数据丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1034">In some instances, a sync-engine backed sharepoint file could show 'Saved' but not have actually saved any changes, resulting in data loss.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1035">解决了用户可能无法保存 Word、Excel 和 PowerPoint 文档的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1035">Resolved an issue where users may be unable to save Word, Excel, and PowerPoint documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1036">此问题会影响创建新文件并在单击“保存”图标或按 Ctrl + S 后显示“另存为对话框”选项的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1036">This issue affects users that create a new file and bring up the "Save as Dialog" option after clicking on the Save icon or pressing Ctrl + S.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1037">通过移出已弃用的 API，修复了 Word 中的崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1037">Fixes a crash in Word by moving away from a deprecated API.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1038">修复了在 PowerPoint 中的竖排文本框中，半角片假名字符未正确旋转的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1038">Fixing an issue where half-width katakana characters were not rotating properly when in vertical text boxes in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1039">修复了 Win7 中的性能问题，它导致所有应用中功能区内的“插入形状”库大约需要 4 秒钟才会显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1039">Fixed a perf issue on Win7 where the insert shapes gallery from the ribbon in all apps took approximately 4 seconds to appear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1040">修复了在后台的信息放置面板中未显示可访问性信息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1040">Fixed a bug where accessibility information was not being displayed in the Info Place slab of the backstage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1041">改进了有关注册表完整性的 Office 更新进程的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1041">Improves reliability of the Office update process concerning registry integrity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1042">我们已将 2019 年 1 月和 7 月分支的频道名称更新为新频道名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1042">We have updated the channel names for the January and July 2019 forks to the new channel names.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1043">更正了按流量计费的网络上可能意外阻止更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1043">Corrects an issue where updates may have been unexpectedly blocked on metered networks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1044">修复了 ODT 和 GPO 更新截止时间设置中相对截止日期仅在第一次设置时起作用，而修复程序为后续更新启用相对截止日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1044">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1045">即在某些情况下，Office 快捷方式可能会在更新后消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1045">In certain circumstances, Office shortcuts may disappear following an update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1046">此更新改进了发布 Office 快捷方式的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1046">This update improves reliability when publishing of Office shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1047">解决了 Office 更新可能已意外地从 Office CDN 而不是计划源（例如本地/网络共享或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置）下载文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1047">Resolves an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1048">解决了以下问题：在某些情况下，如果不是管理员，并且系统帐户没有网络连接，则不会应用更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1048">Resolves an issue where an update would not apply in certain cases where the user is not an administrator and the System account did not have network connectivity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1049">修复了 Office 更新消息以与预期不同的语言显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1049">Fixed an issue where Office update messages appear in a different language than expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1050">今后，Office 更新消息将正确匹配 Windows 显示语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1050">Going forward, Office update messages will correctly match the Windows display language.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1051">通过恢复以前可能已中断的下载，增强了下载 Office 更新时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1051">Improved reliability when downloading Office updates by resuming downloads which may have been previously interrupted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1052">解决了与第三方插件中的“文本框/形状自动调整”属性相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1052">Address issues related to Textbox/Shape Autofit property in third-party plug-ins.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1053">此更改解决了打开损坏的文件后正确呈现图像的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1053">This change addresses correctly rendering images after opening a corrupted file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1054">此更改解决了某些包含标记的散点图呈现缓慢的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1054">This change addresses slow rendering of some scatter charts with markers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1055">我们修复了大型树视图可能会导致崩溃的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1055">We fixed an issue where large tree views could result in a crash</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1056">此更新修复了 Microsoft Office 中 Visual Basic for Applications 的以下问题：某些引用库名称或库路径中包含 DBSC 字符的代码库的 VBA 项目会被 Office 应用程序视为加载时损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1056">This update fixes an issue in Visual Basic for Applications in Microsoft Office where certain VBA projects that contain references to code libraries with DBCS characters in the library name or library path would be viewed by the Office application as corrupt on load.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1057">为了保护 Office 客户的安全，现在仅使用 SHA-2 算法对 Microsoft Office 更新进行签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1057">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1058">为了保护 Office 客户的安全，现在仅使用 SHA-2 算法对 Microsoft Office 更新进行签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1058">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1185">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1185">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1186">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1186">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1187">此更新修复了以下问题：当使用 VBA 向图表的页眉/页脚添加图像时，将会导致出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1187">This update fixes an issue that caused an error to occur whenever VBA was used to add an image to the header/footer of a chart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1188">修复了在打印预览中或打印时分组框控件的边框不可见的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1188">Fixed an issue where the border of a Group Box control wasn't visible in print preview or when printed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1189">用户在使用部分非英文字符集保存更改时可能会出错。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1189">Users may encounter an error when saving changes while using some non-English character sets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1190">修复了以下问题：在保存包含图表的工作簿时，图表标题中的图像文件大小增加。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1190">Fixed an issue where the file size of images in chart headers increased when the workbook containing the chart was saved.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1191">修复了以下问题：在使所选区域与交叉引用的工作簿保持同步时，导致交叉引用工作簿中的 DBCS 字符出现损坏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1191">Fixed an issue that causes corruption of DBCS characters in cross referenced books by keeping the selection ranges in sync with the cross referenced book.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1192">解决了使用自动调整功能调整行高时复选框控件缩小的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1192">Resolved an issue that could cause check box controls to shrink when using autofit to adjust row height.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1193">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1193">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1194">解决了导致用户在指定无效的发件人地址时遇到崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1194">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when specifying an invalid From address.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1195">解决了导致用户在处理冲突消息时遇到同步失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1195">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience sync failures when processing conflict messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1196">解决了导致用户在启动 Outlook 时在“正在加载个人资料”屏幕上遇到挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1196">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a hang at the Loading Profile screen when Outlook is starting up.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1197">解决了导致用户在更改视图时遇到间歇性崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1197">Addressed an issue that caused users to see intermittent crashes when changing views.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1198">解决了导致用户在 Citrix 环境中查看 30 个以上日历时遇到崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1198">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when viewing more than 30 calendars in a Citrix environment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1199">[此处](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3141476/outlook-may-crash-when-you-view-more-than-30-calendars-in-a-calen)是单个 KB，包含针对先前版本记录的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1199">[Here](https://support.microsoft.com/help/3141476/outlook-may-crash-when-you-view-more-than-30-calendars-in-a-calen) is the individual KB where this was documented for previous versions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1200">解决了一个问题，该问题导致用户在将共享日历文件夹同步到 OST 时遇到问题，这导致他们与这些文件夹进行交互时出现权限错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1200">Addresses an issue that caused users to have problems problems with shared calendar folders syncing to the OST, resulting in permission errors when they try to interact with these folders.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1241">**无缝切换：** 新的帐户管理器在同一个位置显示你的所有 Office 365 工作和个人帐户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1241">**Switch seamlessly:** The new account manager shows all of your Office 365 work and personal accounts in one place.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1242">帐户之间可轻松自如切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1242">Switching between them has never been easier.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1243">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1243">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/d17de17e-9f26-4dae-bd08-d7b8f46eb0b9)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1244">**增加内容的覆盖面：** 需要让你的演示文稿易于访问？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1244">**Increase the reach of your content:** Need to make your presentations accessible?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1245">让辅助功能检查器随时进行关注，但不妨碍到你。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1245">Let the accessibility checker keep an eye on it for you, without getting in the way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1246">通过单击“审查”>“检查辅助功能”进行尝试 - 我们在状态栏中找到你需要查看的内容时会通知你。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1246">Try it by clicking Review > Check Accessibility – we’ll tell you when we find something you need to look at in the status bar.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1247">**快速找到文件：** 正在寻找你最近使用过的文件？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1247">**Find that file fast:** Looking for a file you worked on recently?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1248">只需在“文件”>“主页”上的“搜索”框中输入，即可查找要寻找的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1248">Just type in the Search box on the File > Home page to find the file you're looking for.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-p211">**深入发掘数据：** 全新的“想法”按钮可查找数据中的模式并使用这些模式创建智能、个性化的建议。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/3223aab8-f543-4fda-85ed-76bb0295ffc4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-p211">**Discover more about your data:** The new Ideas button looks for patterns in your data, and uses them to create intelligent, personalized suggestions. [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/3223aab8-f543-4fda-85ed-76bb0295ffc4)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1253">**协作更简单：** 共同创作改进意味着使用条件格式、单元格样式等时，所做的更改将与协作者无缝合并。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1253">**Collaboration just got easier:** Co-authoring improvements mean that when working with conditional formatting, cell styles, and more, your changes are merged seamlessly with those of your collaborators.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1254">**在类似列上连接表：** 在比较用于合并表的列时，获取和转换 (Power Query) 现在具有近似文本匹配逻辑（也称为模糊匹配）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1254">**Join tables on similar columns:** Get & Transform (Power Query) now features approximate text matching logic (also called fuzzy matching) when comparing columns for merging tables.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1255">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1255">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/ffdd5082-c0c8-4c8e-a794-bd3962b90649)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1258">**搜索和享受：** 我们添加了“搜索”来插入图标，以便轻松找到所需的图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1258">**Search and enjoy:** We've added Search to Insert Icons to make it easy to find the icon you want.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1259">选择时，“插入”按钮会显示已选数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1259">And when you're selecting, the Insert button tells you how many you've picked.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1260">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1260">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1261">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1261">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1262">**我们已经为你更新了 Outlook 用户体验：** 简化的体验，以前可供预览，现即将推出，旨在帮助你关注最重要的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1262">**We’ve updated the Outlook user experience for you:** A simplified experience, previously available for preview with Coming Soon, designed to help you focus on what matters most.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1263">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1263">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/db503157-1b45-45d5-af52-e9c978cd8bed)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1264">**还可自定义的简化功能区：** 最常用的按钮排成一行，带给你简化体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1264">**A simplified ribbon that's customizable, too:** Enjoy a streamlined, single row of the most frequently used buttons.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1265">可在经典视图和简化视图之间轻松切换，还可固定/取消固定命令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1265">Easily switch between classic and Simplified views, and pin/unpin commands.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1266">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1266">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/44bef9c3-295d-4092-b7f0-f471fa629a98)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1267">**移动邮件时继续工作：** Outlook 现在在后台移动邮件，因此你可以在文件夹之间移动大量邮件时继续工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1267">**Keep working while moving messages:** Outlook now moves messages in the background, so you can keep working while moving lots of messages between folders.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1343">**使用\@提及** 功能引起他人的注意：在批注中使用 @提及，以在需要同事的意见时让他们知悉。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1343">**Get Their Attention with \@Mentions:** Use @mentions in comments to let co-workers know when you need their input.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1344">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1344">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/644bf689-31a0-4977-a4fb-afe01820c1fd)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1345">**搜索和享受：** 我们添加了“搜索以插入图标”，让你能轻松找到所需图标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1345">**Search and enjoy:** We've added Search to Insert Icons to make it easy to find the icon you want.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1346">选择时，“插入”按钮会显示已选数目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1346">And when you're selecting, the Insert button tells you how many you've picked.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1347">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1347">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1348">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1348">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1349">**快速找到文件：** 正在寻找你最近使用过的文件？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1349">**Find that file fast:** Looking for a file you worked on recently?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1350">只需在“文件”>“打开”选项卡上的“搜索”框中输入，即可查找要寻找的文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1350">Just type in the Search box on the File > Open tab to find the file you're looking for.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1351">**在更改时进行保存：** 将文件上传到 OneDrive，以确保所有更新均自动保存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1351">**Save your changes as they happen:** Upload your file to OneDrive to make sure all your updates are saved automatically.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1352">**隐私控制：** 对诊断数据和连接体验的全新、更新和改进控制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1352">**Privacy controls:** New, updated, and improved controls for diagnostic data and connected experiences.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1353">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1353">Learn more</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/privacy/overview-privacy-controls?toc=/deployoffice/toc.json)

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1354">**Office 图标具有新的外观：** Office 图标经过重新设计，可体现简单、强大和智能的 Office 体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1354">**Office icons have a new look:** The Office icons have been redesigned to reflect simple, powerful, and intelligent Office experiences.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1355">**Microsoft Teams 安装：** 默认情况下，将为现已安装的 Office 365 专业增强版安装 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1355">**Installation of Microsoft Teams:** Microsoft Teams is installed by default for existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="630b9-1356">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1356">Learn more</span></span>](https://docs.microsoft.com/DeployOffice/teams-install)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1359">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1359">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1360">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1360">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1361">该更新修复了诸如“总和”等聚合可能将结果截断为整数值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1361">This update fixes an issue where aggregate like Sum may truncate the result to an integer value.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1362">该更新修复了包含对远程表（例如 SQL Server 表）的引用的联合查询可能导致 Access 关闭并重新启动的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1362">This update fixes an issue where a Union query that includes references to remote tables (e.g. SQL Server tables) may cause Access to close and restart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1363">此更新修复了 Microsoft Access 中的一个问题，该问题可能会导致运行更新查询或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 语句时出现&quot;查询已损坏&quot;错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1363">This update fixes an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error &quot;Query is Corrupt&quot; when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1364">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1364">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1365">荷兰语文档标题快捷键提示已更改为 Alt-G。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1365">Dutch keytip for document title has been changed to Alt-G.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1366">修复了 Excel 中的问题，其中分配给形状或表单控件的宏可能显示不正确的错误消息，或者可能在不正确的目标区域中工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1366">Fixed an issue in Excel where macros assigned to shapes or form controls may show incorrect error message, or may work on incorrect target ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1367">解决了一个“查找和替换”问题，即在找到第一个项目后它改变了对话框中焦点的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1367">Resolved an issue with Find and Replace that change where the focus was in the dialog after finding the first item.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1368">修复了在更改数据透视表的排序方式并在与其他用户进行共同创作会话期间刷新它时可能触发崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1368">This fixes an issue where changing the way a PivotTable is sorted and refreshing it while in a coauthoring session with other users could trigger a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1369">我们修复了当 OLAP 数据透视表的筛选器设置为已从多维数据集中删除的值时的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1369">We fixed a problem when the filter for an OLAP PivotTable was set to a value that had been removed from the cube.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1370">修复了使用图表模板插入图表时预览中所用颜色的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1370">Fix to correct colors used in previews when inserting charts using chart templates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1371">我们修复了在更改系列集合时可能导致散点图和折线图无法正确呈现的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1371">We fixed an issue which could have caused scatter line charts from rendering properly when changing the series collection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1372">解决了导致瀑布图和漏斗图无法与插入或删除单元格时的表格同步的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1372">Resolved an issue that caused Waterfall and Funnel charts to get out of sync with tables when cells were inserted or deleted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1373">已修复了 Excel 中的合并冲突问题，该问题会导致系统提示用户重新打开工作簿以使更改生效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1373">Fixed a merge conflict issue in Excel that would result in users being prompted to reopen workbook to pick up the changes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1374">解决了打开嵌入式工作簿时，未加载功能区自定义项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1374">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1375">解决了导致激活最小化窗口的宏运行时错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1375">Resolved an issue that caused a macro run-time error activating minimized windows.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1376">解决了打开嵌入式工作簿时，未加载功能区自定义项的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1376">Resolved an issue with ribbon customization not loading when opening embedded workbook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1377">解决了在与其他人共同创作时导致表旁边的剪切和粘贴操作失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1377">Resolved an issue that caused cut and paste operations next to a table to fail when co-authoring with others.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1378">解决了在使用运行的宏更改自定义属性时导致共同创作中断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1378">Resolved an issue that caused co-authoring interruptions when changing custom properties with running macros.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1379">发生问题时，将无法从加载项打开的 WPF （Windows Presentation Foundation）窗体的组合框中选择项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1379">There was a problem in which you would be unable to select items from combo box of a WPF (Windows Presentation Foundation) form that was opened by an add-in.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1380">解决了在无工作簿打开的情况下搜索最近使用的文件时可能导致出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1380">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1381">异步用户定义函数的性能问题，该问题导致它们同步运行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1381">Performance issue with Asynchronous User-Defined Functions that was causing them to be run Synchronously.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1382">显著提高了删除包含合并单元格的列时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1382">Significant improvements to the performance of deleting columns with merged cells.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1383">解决了在滚动后选择单元格时可能导致选择错误单元格的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1383">Resolved an issue where selecting a cell after scrolling could result in the wrong cell being selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1384">解决了 Lookup 函数可能返回错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1384">Resolved an issue where the Lookup function may return an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1385">解决了一个问题，当创建于早期版本的 Office 中的工作簿在当前版本的 Office 中打开时，可能会导致 Excel 挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1385">Resolved an issue where workbooks created in earlier versions of Office could cause Excel to hang when opened in current versions of Office.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1386">当文件具有大量条件格式时，单击“字体颜色”按钮时会出现性能较低的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1386">Issue with slow performance on clicking on the Font Color button when a file has extensive conditional formatting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1387">我们修复了打印预览中的打印区域不正确的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1387">We fixed an issue where the print area in print preview was not correct.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1388">Excel 可能会在编辑不受信任的网络共享中的受保护文件时遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1388">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1389">我们显著提高了按颜色筛选的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1389">We have significantly improved the performance of filtering by color.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1390">解决了一个阻止将超链接粘贴到某些受保护工作表中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1390">Resolved an issue that prevented Hyperlinks from being pasted in some protected sheets.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1391">在加载项管理器中浏览时允许显示超过 16 个加载项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1391">Enabled more than 16 add-ins to show when browsing in the add-in manager.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1392">此更改通过利用软件呈现避免了某些 Intel 图形驱动程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1392">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1393">Outlook 邮件中的 cid: images 链接现在可以在请求时成功断开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1393">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1394">此更新修复了 Office 文档可能无法上传到 OneDrive for business，同时显示“上传失败”消息的错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1394">This update fixes an error where Office documents may fail to upload to OneDrive for Business with the message "Upload Failed".</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1395">修复了在 Excel 创意功能中发现一个的问题，即通过单击 Win32 客户端中的“创意”按钮加载加载项时出错。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1395">Fix issue in Excel Ideas feature, error when loading the add-in by clicking the Ideas button in Win32 client.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1396">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1396">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1397">Outlook 邮件中的 cid: images 链接现在可以在请求时成功断开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1397">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1398">修复了将邮箱从基本身份验证升级到新式身份验证的用户最终获得与其 Outlook 配置文件关联的错误帐户的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1398">Fixed an issue where users having their mailbox upgraded from basic to modern authentication were ending up with the wrong account associated with their Outlook profile.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1399">解决了导致 Web 加载项在不应该访问“数字版权管理”消息时访问它们的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1399">Addressed an issue that caused web add ins to access Digital Rights Managed messages when they should not.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1400">解决了导致简单悬停 URL 无法显示某些安全链接的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1400">Addressed an issue that caused the simple-hover URLs to fail to display for some safelinks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1401">这将 Outlook 中的附件阻止逻辑更新为也阻止 Python 附件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1401">This updates the attachment blocking logic in Outlook to also block python attachments.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1402">解决了导致部分 POP3 用户看到无论设置如何，其所有电子邮件均采用纯文本格式的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1402">Addressed an issue that caused a subset of POP3 users to see all of their emails formatted at plain text, regardless of settings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1403">此修补程序将还原 HTML 格式邮件的视图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1403">This fix will restore the view of the HTML formatted messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1404">解决了在将用户主日历中的项复制到组日历时出现导致用户遇到权限错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1404">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a permission error when copying items from their primary calendar to a group calendar.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1405">解决了导致用户无法通过屏幕阅读器访问位置建议的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1405">Addressed an issue that caused users to be unable to access location suggestions via a screen reader.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1406">解决了导致用户在通过键盘快捷方式与其邮箱文件夹交互时出现明显延迟的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1406">Addressed an issue that caused users to see a noticeable delay when interacting with their mailbox folders through keyboard shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1407">解决了导致非常长的 Outlook 会话出现内存泄漏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1407">Addressed an issue that caused a memory leak for very long Outlook sessions.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1408">解决了导致用户在打开规则对话框时看到“此计算机上的规则与 Microsoft Exchange 上的规则不匹配”提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1408">Addressed an issue that caused users to see a "The rules on this computer do not match the rules on Microsoft Exchange" prompt when opening the Rules dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1409">解决了导致用户在 Outlook 中与特定安全链接交互时崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1409">Addressed an issue that would cause users to experience a crash in Outlook when interacting with certain safelinks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1410">解决了导致经理不清楚代理人是否已响应指定的会议请求的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1410">Addressed an issue that caused ambiguity for managers around whether or not a delegate had already responded to a given meeting request.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1411">解决了导致用户在处理某些自动发现响应时崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1411">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when processing some AutoDiscover responses.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1412">解决了导致用户在尝试从“帐户创建”上下文联系支持人员时看到带有“确定”按钮的空白消息框的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1412">Addressed an issue that caused users to see an empty message box with an "OK" button when trying to contact support from the Account Creation context.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1413">该更改能够让管理员能够启用策略以便在自动发现身份验证提示中首选提供的帐户电子邮件而不是 UPN。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1413">This change allows administrators to enable a policy to prefer the provided account email in AutoDiscover auth prompts over the UPN.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1414">默认情况下，自动发现优先于帐户 UPN（如果可用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1414">By default, AutoDiscover prefers the account UPN, when available.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1415">解决了导致用户无法在现代组中查看搜索的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1415">Addressed an issue that caused users to see search failing against Modern Groups.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1416">解决了导致 Outlook 用户在某些情况下“需要密码”的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1416">Addressed an issue that caused Outlook users to get stuck in the "Needs Password" state in certain scenarios.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1417">解决了以下问题：用户看到房间被推荐为会议室，然而会议却被安排在会议室不可用时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1417">Addressed an issue that caused users to see room suggestions for meetings that occurred outside of that room's availability hours.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1418">解决了用户在发送加密电子邮件时遇到“不支持加密算法“错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1418">Addressed an issue that caused users to encounter "encryption algorithm is not supported" errors when sending an encrypted email.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1419">解决了非英语用户邮件中的主题行非常小的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1419">Addressed an issue for non-English users where the subject line in a mail would be incredibly small.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1420">解决了导致某些用户在添加辅助 Exchange 帐户时会看到创建重复的特殊文件夹的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1420">Addressed an issue that caused some users to see duplicate special folders created when adding a secondary Exchange account.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1421">解决了导致用户尝试“从错过的对话”消息创建规则时遇到崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1421">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when attempting to create a rule from a "Missed Conversation" message.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1422">解决了 SMIME 算法选择方面的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1422">Corrected an issue with SMIME algorithm selection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1423">解决了在使用备用发件人时导致无法显示策略提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1423">Addressed an issue that caused Policy Tips to fail to display when using an alternate sender.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1424">解决了导致用户在 Outlook 进程中观察到内存泄漏的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1424">Addressed an issue that caused users to observe a memory leak in the Outlook process.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1425">解决了导致用户在更新状态信息时遇到间歇性崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1425">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience intermittent crashes when updating presence information.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1426">解决了导致当前文件夹搜索间歇性失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1426">Addressed an issue that caused current folder search to intermittently fail.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1427">解决了导致某些用户在尝试检索 Outlook 的云设置时遇到身份验证错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1427">Addressed an issue that caused some users to encounter authentication errors when trying to retrieve their cloud settings for Outlook.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1428">解决了导致“搜索反馈”体验挂起的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1428">Addressed an issue that caused a hang in the Search Feedback experience.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1429">解决了导致用户在处理某些自动发现响应时崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1429">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when processing some AutoDiscover responses.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1430">解决了导致用户在更新状态信息时遇到间歇性崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1430">Addressed an issue that caused users to experience intermittent crashes when updating presence information.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1431">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1431">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1432">修复了某些加载项会在图表中的形状周围引发意外错误的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1432">Fixed an issue where some add-ins would throw unexpected errors around shapes in charts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1433">Outlook 邮件中的 cid: images 链接现在可以在请求时成功断开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1433">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1434">该更改还原 PowerPoint 视频控件易于访问的名称。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1434">This change restores the accessible name for PowerPoint video controls.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1435">我们修复了可能阻止某些动画启动的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1435">We fixed an issue which could prevent some animations from starting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1436">我们修复了将一个幻灯片从一个演示文稿复制到另一个演示文稿时，可能创建重复母版的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1436">We fixed an issue when copying a slide from one presentation to another might create duplicate masters.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1437">如果在不支持的版本中打开，采用新批注的文件将显示黄色警告</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1437">Files with new modern comments will show a yellow warning if opened in unsupported version</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1438">可靠性修复：修复了第三方加载项可能导致 PowerPoint 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1438">Reliability fix: Fixed an issue where third party add-in might crash PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1439">修复了在 PowerPoint 中的竖排文本框中，半角片假名字符未正确旋转的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1439">Fixed an issue where half-width katakana characters were not rotating properly when in vertical text boxes in PowerPoint.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1440">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1440">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1441">修复了 Windows 7 上的用户能够从 Project Web App 和 SharePoint 网站打开项目的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1441">Fixed an issue to enable users on Windows 7 to be able to open projects from Project Web App and SharePoint sites.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1442">发现了用户在打开只读项目时可能会收到几则消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1442">Identified an issue where users could get several messages when opening a read-only project.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1443">“全部调配”命令不能正确解决资源的过度分配。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1443">Level All command doesn't properly resolve a resource overallocation.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1444">如果你的任务分配为零工作，该任务可能无法标记为已完成，并且始终显示为 99%。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1444">An assignment with zero work on a task, the task may be unable to be marked complete and will always show up at 99%.</span></span>

### <a name="visio"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1445">Visio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1445">Visio</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1446">从 Visio 导出为 SVG 的操作无法用于各种形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1446">Export as SVG from Visio was failing for a variety of shapes.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1447">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1447">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1448">此更改将提升使用 Word 打开文档的效率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1448">This change will lead to performance improvements in opening documents using Word.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1449">Outlook 邮件中的 cid: images 链接现在可以在请求时成功断开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1449">The links of cid: images from Outlook messages can now be successfully broken when requested.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1450">我们修复了在使用 Deskjet 打印机打印时可能导致缩放问题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1450">We fixed an issue which could have caused scaling issues when printing to Deskjet printers.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1451">我们修复了跟踪更改有时会陷入无限循环的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1451">We fixed an issue in track changes that sometimes go into infinite loop.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1452">修复了应用可能会在关闭时挂起的各种问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1452">Fixed various issues where the app may hang on shutdown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1453">还修复了某些加载项相关的崩溃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1453">Also fixes certain add-in related crashes.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="630b9-1454">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1454">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1455">修复了将采用平假名和日语汉字的新纪元名称“Reiwa”错误地标识为拼写错误或不符合语法的表达式的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1455">Fixed an issue of incorrectly identifying the new era name “Reiwa” in Hiragana and Kanji as a misspelled or ungrammatical expression.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1456">修复了一个问题，该问题导致用户在尝试共享存储在 SharePoint 2016 上的文件时收到消息“抱歉，无法我们共享此内容”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1456">Fixed an issue which caused users to get this message "Sorry, something is preventing us from sharing this" when trying to share files stored on SharePoint 2016.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1457">修复了可能会导致 PowerPoint 中涉及共同创作和脱机编辑的会话中数据丢失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1457">Fixed issue that could cause data loss in sessions that involved both coauthoring and offline editing in PowerPoint.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1458">此修复可解决用户打开文件时可能遇到的崩溃问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1458">This is a fix for a crash that users could hit on opening a file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1459">防止 PowerPoint 用户在尝试联机演示时遇到错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1459">Prevents PowerPoint users from running into error when trying to Present Online.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1460">在某些情况下，同步引擎支持的 sharepoint 文件可能显示“已保存”，但并未真正保存任何更改，导致数据丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1460">In some instances, a sync-engine backed sharepoint file could show 'Saved' but not have actually saved any changes, resulting in data loss.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1461">解决了用户可能无法保存 Word、Excel 和 PowerPoint 文档的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1461">Resolved an issue where users may be unable to save Word, Excel, and PowerPoint documents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1462">此问题会影响创建新文件并在单击“保存”图标或按 Ctrl + S 后显示“另存为对话框”选项的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1462">This issue affects users that create a new file and bring up the "Save as Dialog" option after clicking on the Save icon or pressing Ctrl + S.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1463">修复了 Win7 中的性能问题，它导致所有应用中功能区内的“插入形状”库大约需要 4 秒钟才会显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1463">Fixed a perf issue on Win7 where the insert shapes gallery from the ribbon in all apps took approximately 4 seconds to appear.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1464">修复了在后台的信息放置面板中未显示可访问性信息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1464">Fixed a bug where accessibility information was not being displayed in the Info Place slab of the backstage.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1465">改进了有关注册表完整性的 Office 更新进程的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1465">Improves reliability of the Office update process concerning registry integrity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1466">解决了 Office 更新可能已意外地从 Office CDN 而不是计划源（例如本地/网络共享或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置）下载文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1466">Resolved an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1467">修复了 Office 更新消息以与预期不同的语言显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1467">Fixed an issue where Office update messages appear in a different language than expected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1468">今后，Office 更新消息将正确匹配 Windows 显示语言。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1468">Going forward, Office update messages will correctly match the Windows display language.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1469">解决了以下问题：在某些情况下，如果不是管理员，并且系统帐户没有网络连接，则不会应用更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1469">Resolved an issue where an update would not apply in certain cases where the user is not an administrator and the System account did not have network connectivity.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1470">即在某些情况下，Office 快捷方式可能会在更新后消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1470">In certain circumstances, Office shortcuts may disappear following an update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1471">此更新改进了发布 Office 快捷方式的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1471">This update improves reliability when publishing of Office shortcuts.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1472">更正了按流量计费的网络上可能意外阻止更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1472">Corrected an issue where updates may have been unexpectedly blocked on metered networks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1473">修复了 ODT 和 GPO 更新截止时间设置中相对截止日期仅在第一次设置时起作用，而修复程序为后续更新启用相对截止日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1473">Fix to bug in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1474">通过恢复以前可能已中断的下载，增强了下载 Office 更新时的可靠性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1474">Improved reliability when downloading Office updates by resuming downloads which may have been previously interrupted.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1475">解决了与第三方插件中的“文本框/形状自动调整”属性相关的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1475">Addressed issues related to Textbox/Shape Autofit property in third-party plug-ins.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1476">我们修复了大型树视图可能会导致崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1476">We fixed an issue where large tree views could result in a crash.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="630b9-1477">为了保护 Office 客户的安全，现在仅使用 SHA-2 算法对 Microsoft Office 更新进行签名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="630b9-1477">To protect Office customers' security, Microsoft Office updates are now signed using the SHA-2 algorithm exclusively.</span></span>
